\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/5d13b00bca651227eb55616363f7d7eb8a91f8e8}{\texttt{ 5d13b00}}) fix(jasmine)\+: Update Jasmine to support Node8 async/await (\#4608)

Breaking change for Type\+Script\+: Jasmine\+WD doesn\textquotesingle{}t know anything about async/await, turns off Jasmine\+WD if control flow was disabled.

It will affect Type\+Script tests that are using async/await and

a. miss some await keyword in the test.(Previously, this might cause the test failed silently and be reported as pass), or

b. use Promise in jasmine expect function

{\bfseries{Before}} \`{}\`{}\`{}ts await expect(get\+Promise()).to\+Equal(42); \`{}\`{}\`{} {\bfseries{After}} \`{}\`{}\`{}ts expect(await get\+Promise()).to\+Equal(42); \`{}\`{}\`{}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33073}{}\doxysection{5.\+2.\+0}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33073}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33083}{}\doxysubsection{Breaking Changes}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33083}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The protocol for a Sauce Labs selenium relay (sauce\+Selenium\+Address in protractor.\+conf.\+js) is \textquotesingle{}https\textquotesingle{} (previously used \textquotesingle{}http\textquotesingle{}). The protocol is not configurable in this version.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33084}{}\doxysection{5.\+1.\+0}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33084}
\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33085}{}\doxyparagraph{Blocking proxy}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33085}
Blocking Proxy is a new experimental feature in Protractor 5 and is behind the {\ttfamily -\/-\/use\+Blocking\+Proxy} or {\ttfamily blocking\+Proxy\+Url}. See the \href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/blob/master/lib/config.ts\#L100}{\texttt{ lib/config.\+ts\#\+L100}}. Other ways to start blocking proxy include using the {\ttfamily -\/-\/highlight\+Delay} and {\ttfamily -\/-\/web\+Driver\+Log\+Dir} flags See \href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/blob/master/lib/config.ts\#L501}{\texttt{ lib/config.\+ts\#\+L501}}.

This adds two options, both of which are implemented with Blocking Proxy. {\ttfamily -\/-\/web\+Driver\+Log\+Dir} will create a readable log with timing information of webdriver commands in the specified directory.

{\ttfamily -\/-\/highlight\+Delay} will pause before clicking on elements or sending keys. While paused, the element that\textquotesingle{}s about to be affected will be highlighted.\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33086}{}\doxyparagraph{Webdriver-\/manager}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33086}
Webdriver-\/manager will now by default grab the latest versions of all binaries (standalone, chromedriver, iedriver, gecko driver). Use the {\ttfamily -\/-\/versions.(binary name)} to pin to a specific version. Selenium standalone 3.\+0.\+1 has a bug which prevents it from working with any version of Fire\+Fox. We have tested version 3.\+0.\+0-\/beta4 and know that it works with Fire\+Fox 51, and we expect that the 3.\+0.\+2 release will also work.\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33087}{}\doxyparagraph{Type\+Script support}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33087}
For jasmine users, in order to get all the type declarations that are used in jasminewd2, you\textquotesingle{}ll need to install {\ttfamily @types/jasminewd2} in addition to {\ttfamily @types/jasmine} as dev dependencies.\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33088}{}\doxysubsection{Features}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33088}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/0cd156d6829f23f93403d865b7fdb7eab4f45446}{\texttt{ 0cd156d}}) feat(debugging)\+: Add webdriver logging and highlight delay. (\#4039)

This adds two options, both of which are implemented with Blocking Proxy. --web\+Driver\+Log\+Dir will create a readable log with timing information of webdriver commands in the specified directory.

--highlight\+Delay will pause before clicking on elements or sending keys. While paused, the element that\textquotesingle{}s about to be affected will be highlighted.

\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/7cb9739954bc26f0667d671cdb0083f5bd43f2f6}{\texttt{ 7cb9739}}) feat(browser.\+ready)\+: make {\ttfamily browser.\+ready} wait for all async setup work (\#4015)

\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/b77cb928301fbe4f77ffcdcace424a490581416e}{\texttt{ b77cb92}}) feat(restart)\+: {\ttfamily browser.\+restart} should return a promise (\#4008)

Also allows {\ttfamily browser.\+restart} to work when the control flow is disabled, and fixes it for forked browsers.

Closes \#3899 and \#3896 \href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/issues/3896}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/issues/3896}}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/4a59412357eb5df592b06dd282d88d6dbc5e4771}{\texttt{ 4a59412}}) feat(angular\+App\+Root)\+: Replace root\+El with browser.\+angular\+App\+Root() (\#3996)

Replace browser.\+root\+El with browser.\+angular\+App\+Root(), which changes the root element in a promise on the control flow. Note that browser.\+root\+El will immediately return the current value, but browser.\+angular\+App\+Root() will return a promise that resolves during the next step in the control flow.

Also update to Blocking\+Proxy 0.\+0.\+3, which allows changing root\+Selector.
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/879aac6ee6c1c36d005b538472e2754b987b3368}{\texttt{ 879aac6}}) chore(blockingproxy)\+: Allow using a pre-\/existing Blocking Proxy instance (\#3970)
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/bf123adafc442440b2ca10725113b47342ebb24f}{\texttt{ bf123ad}}) feat(elements)\+: Add is\+Present() to Element\+Array\+Finder. (\#3974)
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33089}{}\doxysubsection{Bug Fixes}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33089}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/f9bee84bc03b6cd6872522b8780327423b789e19}{\texttt{ f9bee84}}) fix(restart)\+: preserve wait\+For\+Angular\+Enabled on restart and add promise chaining

I noticed I missed {\ttfamily wait\+For\+Angular\+Enabled} in \#4037. This commit fixed that.

While I was at it I fixed a minor error where the promises implicitly created by setting {\ttfamily root\+El} and {\ttfamily ignore\+Synchronization} weren\textquotesingle{}t getting chained properly.

Also fixed minor (so minor I think it was impossible to trigger) where browser.\+plugins\+\_\+ could be undefined.
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/0b0c224e4056368c2c0030064b4ca4235163276b}{\texttt{ 0b0c224}}) fix(plugins)\+: do not force Managed\+Promise in plugins.\+ts (\#4036)
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/9c2274d8f218cabc946dbc6a11d725458c1b4e3a}{\texttt{ 9c2274d}}) fix(restart)\+: preserve properties like {\ttfamily browser.\+base\+Url} upon restart (\#4037)

I also fixed a minor issue where {\ttfamily internal\+Root\+El} wasn\textquotesingle{}t being set when blocking proxy was being used. I also just cleaned up our internal uses of {\ttfamily this.\+root\+El}.

Closes \#4032
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/a20c7a7cc1df04f96cb1a9dd971df39883ac173b}{\texttt{ a20c7a7}}) fix(element chaining)\+: make element chaining work when the control flow is disabled (\#4029)

Also added some tests to {\ttfamily spec/ts/no\+CF/smoke\+\_\+spec.\+ts} double checking that the control flow is off
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/7481dee75cab1da9d207909e928eee55a9f5a682}{\texttt{ 7481dee}}) fix(cli)\+: Make unknown flag check a warning instead of an error. (\#4028)
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/40bbeca003017901760e10831c66d383cf5accf8}{\texttt{ 40bbeca}}) fix(expected\+Conditions)\+: Add tests and fix race conditions around visibility (\#4006)

Add test cases to reproduce the missing element race conditions possible in expected condition methods {\ttfamily visibility\+Of}, {\ttfamily text\+To\+Be\+Present\+In\+Element}, {\ttfamily text\+To\+Be\+Present\+In\+Value} and {\ttfamily element\+To\+Be\+Clickable}.

Add error handler {\ttfamily false\+If\+Missing} to all expected conditions that depend on the presence of an element.

Expected conditions check the presence of an element before other checks, but when an element is removed exactly in the moment after the {\ttfamily is\+Present} and before {\ttfamily is\+Displayed} in {\ttfamily visibility\+Of} the condition used to fail.

This solution does not handle missing elements in ({\ttfamily is\+Enable}, {\ttfamily is\+Displayed}, {\ttfamily is\+Selected}) and focused only on expected conditions (see \#3972)

This problem was also referenced in \#3578 and \#3777
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/5856037368ee8d8a21f11eadbfe93d5f46507f60}{\texttt{ 5856037}}) fix(cli)\+: Allow frameworks to specify flags they recognize. (\#3994)

Fix for \#3978. Our initial plan to allow setting --disable\+Checks with an environment variable is insufficient, since the custom framework isn\textquotesingle{}t even require()\textquotesingle{}d until after the config is parsed. This moves the unknown flag check into the runner, and gives frameworks a way to specify extra flags they accept.
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/e68dcf1bfd7f32c59ebd23fa16ca53e1a53f8ddf}{\texttt{ e68dcf1}}) fix(driver\+Providers)\+: Check config in the right place. (\#3991)
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/eb899208457f83853f043edea5e56b07e87803bc}{\texttt{ eb89920}}) fix(driver\+Providers)\+: Handle promise rejection when starting selenium (\#3989)

Fixes \#3986. Also error if jvm\+Args isn\textquotesingle{}t an array.
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/8d2fc07ed28a1b19c03a9869442f76f2963e40a1}{\texttt{ 8d2fc07}}) chore(browser)\+: deprecate {\ttfamily browser.\+get\+Location\+Abs\+Url()}. (\#3969)

Closes \#3185
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/15a187204bb8b87255d5f4622094eabc71206315}{\texttt{ 15a1872}}) fix(firefox)\+: Fix direct\+Connect for Firefox 51+ (\#3953)
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/81f56a449f8988feba21617ef7533cfa2f06c6f8}{\texttt{ 81f56a4}}) fix(cli)\+: display disable\+Checks option in extra flags error message (\#3964)
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/6a4dc7a6a5b796e0215e5b9abf99494ac13cb647}{\texttt{ 6a4dc7a}}) fix\+: no longer use es6 let statement (\#3963)
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Currently in Protractor v5 the Angular detection script uses ES6 features like the {\ttfamily let} modifier.
\end{DoxyItemize}

This can break Protractor on browsers, which doesn\textquotesingle{}t support those statements. \begin{quote}
See \href{https://saucelabs.com/beta/tests/275f75091dac40a0a3374d29d912caee/commands\#11}{\texttt{ https\+://saucelabs.\+com/beta/tests/275f75091dac40a0a3374d29d912caee/commands\#11}} \end{quote}

\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/528338c6722219fdcfc51153b0031a02f0fce046}{\texttt{ 528338c}}) fix(expected\+Condition)\+: fix No\+Such\+Element\+Error in visibility\+Of due to a race condition (\#3777)

Handle No\+Such\+Element\+Error in the expected condition visibility\+Of, which occurred when an element disappears between the is\+Present() and is\+Displayed() check.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33090}{}\doxysubsection{Dependencies}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33090}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/5899b676bc2db0005506ae2306350e6ffea3c808}{\texttt{ 5899b67}}) deps(update)\+: update webdriver-\/manager to $^\wedge$12.0.\+1 (\#4042)

Running {\ttfamily webdriver-\/manager update} will now by default grab the latest versions of all binaries (standalone, chromedriver, iedriver, gecko driver). You can continue to pin to a specific versions using the command line option. Example {\ttfamily webdriver-\/manager update -\/-\/versions.\+chrome 2.\+20}. As of this release the latest versions are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item gecko v0.\+14.\+0
\item selenium-\/standalone 3.\+0.\+1 is the latest jar file; however, we recommend 3.\+0.\+0-\/beta4. See note below on Firefox support.
\item chromedriver 2.\+27
\item iedriver 3.\+0.\+0

A note on Fire\+Fox support\+: Selenium standalone 3.\+0.\+1 has a bug which prevents it from working with any version of Fire\+Fox. We have tested version 3.\+0.\+0-\/beta4 and know that it works with Fire\+Fox 51, and we expect that the 3.\+0.\+2 release will also work.

closes \#4033
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/cd084a0ca29cd73aa3ce1650188adf7ddfdb7962}{\texttt{ cd084a0}}) deps(jasmine)\+: update jasmine to $^\wedge$2.5.\+3 (\#3960)
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33091}{}\doxysection{5.\+0.\+0}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33091}
This version includes big changes around upgrading to selenium-\/webdriver 3.\+0.\+x. See the \href{https://github.com/SeleniumHQ/selenium/blob/master/javascript/node/selenium-webdriver/CHANGES.md}{\texttt{ selenium-\/webdriver changelog}}.

For the 5.\+0.\+0 release, we are still using the selenium standalone server 2.\+53.\+1 and recommend using Firefox 47. Firefox 48+ currently is not supported.\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33092}{}\doxysubsection{Breaking Changes}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33092}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Minimum node version is now 6.\+9.\+x.
\item When testing with Firefox 47, use the capability option {\ttfamily marionette\+: false} to use the legacy Firefox driver.

Before\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{capabilities: \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  browserName: 'firefox'}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


After\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{capabilities: \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  browserName: 'firefox',}
\DoxyCodeLine{  marionette: false}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item We moved {\ttfamily @types/jasmine} to a dev\+Dependency. This means that Jasmine Type\+Script users will need to include the {\ttfamily @types/jasmine} as a project dependency. This is to avoid conflicts for users that prefer mocha typings.

After\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{"{}dependencies"{}: \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  "{}@types/jasmine"{}: "{}\string^2.5.38"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item Selenium-\/webdriver methods removed\+: {\ttfamily Web\+Driver.\+prototype.\+is\+Element\+Present}, {\ttfamily Web\+Element.\+prototype.\+get\+Raw\+Id}, {\ttfamily Web\+Element.\+prototype.\+get\+Inner\+Html}, and {\ttfamily Web\+Element.\+prototype.\+get\+Outer\+Html}.

Before\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{let isPresent = browser.driver.isElementPresent(By.tagName('a'));}
\DoxyCodeLine{let i = element(locator).getInnerHtml();}
\DoxyCodeLine{let o = element(locator).getOuterHtml();}

\end{DoxyCode}


After\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{let isPresent = element(By.tagName('a')).isPresent();}
\DoxyCodeLine{let i = browser.executeScript("{}return arguments[0].innerHTML;"{}, element(locator));}
\DoxyCodeLine{let o = browser.executeScript("{}return arguments[0].outerHTML;"{}, element(locator));}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item Selenium-\/webdriver {\ttfamily Error\+Codes} have been removed.
\item Adding cookies have been changed\+:

Before\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{browser.manage().addCookie('testcookie', 'Jane-\/1234');}

\end{DoxyCode}


After\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{browser.manage().addCookie(\{name:'testcookie', value: 'Jane-\/1234'\});}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item Removed {\ttfamily protractor.\+wrap\+Driver()}.
\item You can no longer use {\ttfamily repl} command from within {\ttfamily browser.\+pause()}. Instead, use {\ttfamily browser.\+explore()} to directly enter the {\ttfamily repl}.
\item Sending flags that are not recognized by the CLI throws an error. Since flags are a subset of all configuration options, these errors can be silenced with {\ttfamily -\/-\/disable\+Checks}.
\item Auto-\/detection of the root element. This is a breaking change because it changes the default root element behavior and removes the {\ttfamily config.\+use\+All\+Angular2\+App\+Roots} flag. Modern angular apps now default to using all app hooks, and ng1 apps now check several places, notably the element the app bootstraps to.
\item {\ttfamily sauce\+Proxy} configuration field has been removed. Use {\ttfamily web\+Driver\+Proxy} instead.

Before\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{sauceProxy: 'http://sauceProxy'}

\end{DoxyCode}


After\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{webDriverProxy: 'http://sauceProxy'}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33093}{}\doxysubsection{Features}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33093}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/ec93c4ab882991410ad9d3f52d87c0f5ec947641}{\texttt{ ec93c4a}}) chore(cli)\+: {\bfseries{breaking change}} throw errors on unknown flags (\#3921)

Unknown flags are options sent that is unrecognized by the CLI. For users that encounter this error but would like to silence it, use\+: {\ttfamily -\/-\/disable\+Checks}.

closes \#3216
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/bc583321a233453fc2b89472013b2ec3e1d6b6f9}{\texttt{ bc58332}}) feat(root\+El)\+: {\itshape {\bfseries{breaking change}}} auto-\/detect the root element better (\#3928)

This is a breaking change because it changes the default root element behavior and removes the {\ttfamily config.\+use\+All\+Angular2\+App\+Roots} flag. Modern angular apps now default to using all app hooks, and ng1 apps now check several places, notably the element the app bootstraps to.

closes \#1742
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/604fdbf064cc2785a2e745747beeaeb45d27f8ed}{\texttt{ 604fdbf}}) cleanup(config)\+: {\bfseries{breaking change}} Remove redundant sauce\+Proxy config (\#3868)

Removes the {\ttfamily sauce\+Proxy} config field, and uses {\ttfamily web\+Driver\+Proxy} when creating the Sauce\+Labs client.
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/9465b9f1e667c9590e05d9ddac16fe5143aa93af}{\texttt{ 9465b9f}}) feat(mobile)\+: add extended wd commands for appium (\#3860)

Also had to make some minor changes to the website to handle longer inheritance chains Closes \href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/issues/1940}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/issues/1940}}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/0e26b218d5f385dd9871a40553acc174cfdfe26d}{\texttt{ 0e26b21}}) feat(blockingproxy)\+: Add synchronization with Blocking\+Proxy. (\#3813)

This adds support for Blocking\+Proxy behind the flag --use\+Blocking\+Proxy.

If set, the driver providers will start a proxy during their setup phase, passing the selenium address to the proxy and starting a webdriver client that talks to the proxy.

Starting a proxy for each driver provider isn\textquotesingle{}t strictly necessary. However, when we run with multiple capabilities it\textquotesingle{}s easier to handle the logging if each Protractor instance has it\textquotesingle{}s own proxy.

Known issues\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Doesn\textquotesingle{}t work with direct\+Connect. You can get the address of chromedriver by mucking around in Selenium internals, but this probably changed for Selenium 3.\+0 and I doubt it\textquotesingle{}s worth figuring out until we upgrade.
\item Doesn\textquotesingle{}t yet work with web\+Driver\+Proxy (but it\textquotesingle{}s an easy fix)
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/ca4f1acda3672942307d0f102d586c8889dd3d68}{\texttt{ ca4f1ac}}) chore(driver\+Providers)\+: add warnings to extra driver provider parameters (\#3873)
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item builds the driver provider in lib/driver\+Providers/index instead of lib/runner closes \#1945
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/681b54a21ee1467d5a95c3693cde148759767d62}{\texttt{ 681b54a}}) refactor(browser)\+: Remove protractor.\+wrap\+Driver() {\bfseries{breaking change}} (\#3827)

Before\+:

Users could create their own selenium driver instance and enable Protractor on it like so\+:
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{let capabilities = webdriver.Capabilities.chrome();}
\DoxyCodeLine{let driver = new webdriver.Builder().usingServer(seleniumAddress)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  .withCapabilities(capabilities).build();}
\DoxyCodeLine{let browser = protractor.wrapDriver(driver);}

\end{DoxyCode}


Over the years, wrap\+Driver() has become increasingly broken as Protractor needs extra configuration options that wrap\+Driver() doesn\textquotesingle{}t set.

After\+:

This method is removed. If users need a new browser instance, they can use {\ttfamily browser.\+fork\+New\+Driver\+Instance()}.

\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/cb38ed0a8aae2cb862001e0b6f076aa9972f4489}{\texttt{ cb38ed0}}) Refactor element explorer to work with selenium-\/webdriver 3 (\#3828)

This implementation now relies mostly on promises explicitly, so the control flow is only used to add one large task to the queue. This should pave the way for the eventual removal of the control flow, as well as getting element explorer to work immediately.

BREAKING CHANGE

You can no longer use the {\ttfamily repl} command from within {\ttfamily browser.\+pause()}. Instead, use {\ttfamily browser.\+explore()} to directly enter the repl.

\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/397bf65e088b640cf3612f9da678180f49939b84}{\texttt{ 397bf65}}) deps(update)\+: move @types/jasmine to dev\+Dependencies (\#3795)

\item move @types/jasmine to dev\+Dependencies closes \#3792
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/a3e8b4319d3e8b049e55e5c3c64a7fdb5a132ddf}{\texttt{ a3e8b43}}) deps(selenium-\/webdriver)\+: upgrade to selenium 3 (\#3781)

Please see the \href{https://github.com/SeleniumHQ/selenium/blob/master/javascript/node/selenium-webdriver/CHANGES.md}{\texttt{ selenium-\/webdriver changelog}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Removed method {\ttfamily Web\+Driver.\+prototype.\+is\+Element\+Present}
\item Removed method {\ttfamily Web\+Element.\+prototype.\+get\+Raw\+Id}
\item Removed {\ttfamily get\+Inner\+Html} and {\ttfamily get\+Outter\+Html}
\item Dependency required for upgrade\+: use {\ttfamily jasminewd2@0.\+1.\+0}.
\item Selenium-\/webdriver requires node version 6+, updating travis and circle yml to use node 6 and 7.
\item Use {\ttfamily instanceof} selenium-\/webdriver error instead of error code. Selenium-\/webdriver error codes have been deprecated.
\item Use executor with selenium-\/webdriver from {\ttfamily lib/http}. Deferred executor has been deprecated.
\item Fix quitting {\ttfamily driver\+Providers}. When calling {\ttfamily webdriver.\+quit}, the control flow is shutdown and will throw an error.
\item Driver provider for direct connect has been modified to use {\ttfamily Service\+Builder} and to call the {\ttfamily Service} to {\ttfamily create\+Session}
\item Note\+: Since this upgrade is still using FF 47, direct connect for Firefox is required to pass \char`\"{}marionette\+: false\char`\"{} in the capabilities. If you do not pass marionette to false, it will look for gecko driver in the PATH.
\item Added a TODO to support FF after 48+ with direct connect and gecko driver.
\item Updated `browser.\+manage().add\+Cookie(\textquotesingle{}testcookie', \textquotesingle{}Jane-\/1234\textquotesingle{});{\ttfamily to use }browser.\+manage().add\+Cookie(\{name\+:\textquotesingle{}testcookie\textquotesingle{}, value\+: \textquotesingle{}Jane-\/1234\textquotesingle{}\});\`{}
\item Updated debug commons for breakpoint updated to selenium-\/webdriver {\ttfamily lib/http} line 432.
\item For mocha tests, {\ttfamily selenium-\/webdriver/testing} uses the global {\ttfamily it} and cannot be reassigned as Protractor\textquotesingle{}s global {\ttfamily it}. Some code has been copied / modified to {\ttfamily lib/frameworks/mocha} to make this work.
\item Capabilities for Firefox 47 requires setting marionette to false.
\item Setup still requires selenium standalone server 2.\+53.\+1 for Firefox tests. Firefox version used is 47.
\item Using selenium standalone server 3, with Firefox 48+ tests fail with gecko driver still do not work.
\item Selenium standalone 3 + FF 49 + gecko driver 0.\+11.\+1 does not work
\item Selenium standalone 3 + FF 48 + gecko driver 0.\+11.\+1 appears to work for a single test but after it quits, selenium standalone no longer works with firefox. When firefox 48 exists, logs show the following\+:

\`{}\`{}\`{} 20\+:01\+:14.\+814 INFO -\/ Executing\+: \mbox{[}delete session\+: e353fa1b-\/e266-\/4ec3-\/afb3-\/88f11a82473a\mbox{]}) \mbox{[}GFX1-\/\mbox{]}\+: Receive IPC close with reason=Abnormal\+Shutdown \mbox{[}Child 30665\mbox{]} \#\#\#!!! ABORT\+: Aborting on channel error.\+: file /builds/slave/m-\/rel-\/m64-\/00000000000000000000/build/src/ipc/glue/\+Message\+Channel.cpp, line 2052 \mbox{[}Child 30665\mbox{]} \#\#\#!!! ABORT\+: Aborting on channel error.\+: file /builds/slave/m-\/rel-\/m64-\/00000000000000000000/build/src/ipc/glue/\+Message\+Channel.cpp, line 2052 \`{}\`{}\`{}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/eb31c9c7755399bcd01630158d900e0b940e9c31}{\texttt{ eb31c9c}}) deps(types)\+: update @types/selenium-\/webdriver dependency (\#3886)

Fixes issue \#3879 and adds the protractor.\+Key.\+chord method

This version includes a breaking change to the Type\+Script import statement. Please see the feature below.\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33113}{}\doxysubsection{Features}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33113}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/5034c89242794dd14aba294ba3468937e06a7b69}{\texttt{ 5034c89}}) feat(typescript)\+: move typescript variable instances from protractor/ (\#3565)

Breaking change for Type\+Script\+: Instead of importing globals like {\ttfamily browser} from {\ttfamily protractor/globals}, import from {\ttfamily protractor}.

Before\+:
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{import \{browser, element\} from 'protractor/globals';}
\DoxyCodeLine{import \{ElementFinder\} from 'protractor';}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{describe('my app', () => \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  myElement: ElementFinder;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  beforeEach(() => \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{    browser.get('example.com');}
\DoxyCodeLine{    myElement = element(by.css('foo'));}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\});}

\end{DoxyCode}


After


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{import \{browser, element, ElementFinder\} from 'protractor';}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{describe('my app', () => \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  myElement: ElementFinder;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  beforeEach(() => \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{    browser.get('example.com');}
\DoxyCodeLine{    myElement = element(by.css('foo'));}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\});}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33122}{}\doxysection{4.\+0.\+5}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33122}
In this version, there are several small changes that affect Type\+Script users from the previous version 4.\+0.\+4. Here are some of the steps to resolve any transpiling errors\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item In your package.\+json, use Type\+Script 2.\+0.\+0. This will allow Protractor to use the {\ttfamily @types/node} and {\ttfamily @types/jasmine} installed in node\+\_\+modules.
\item Remove {\ttfamily jasmine} and {\ttfamily node} from your {\ttfamily typings.\+json} since these types are already included via {\ttfamily @types}. If these were the only ambient typings installed, remove the {\ttfamily typings.\+json} file.
\item If you still have a {\ttfamily typings.\+json} file, remove {\ttfamily typings} directory and install a fresh set of ambient typings with\+: {\ttfamily typings install}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33123}{}\doxysubsection{Features}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33123}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33124}{}\doxysubsection{Bug fixes}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33124}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33134}{}\doxysection{4.\+0.\+0}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33134}
This version includes some big changes, so we\textquotesingle{}ve decided to make it version 4.\+0!


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item webdriver-\/manager is now it\textquotesingle{}s \href{https://www.npmjs.com/package/webdriver-manager}{\texttt{ own NPM}}, so you can use it in your own projects. Protractor depends on it, though, so you shouldn\textquotesingle{}t need to change anything. However, because it is a new dependency you\textquotesingle{}ll need to rerun {\ttfamily webdriver-\/manager update}.
\item Protractor has Type\+Script typings! See the \href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/tree/master/exampleTypescript}{\texttt{ example}} for details on how to use Type\+Script in your tests.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33135}{}\doxysubsection{Breaking changes}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33135}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/d932ad7e853c0bda5d45b478a5c0271d072b6794}{\texttt{ d932ad7}}) chore(browser)\+: rename protractor to browser and add a protractor namespace (\#3214)
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item added wrap\+Driver method from the browser.\+ts and Expected\+Conditions to the protractor namespace
\item imported selenium webdriver Action\+Sequence, Key, promise, Command, and Command\+Name to the protractor namespace
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Selenium Webdriver has deprecated get\+Inner\+Html and get\+Outer\+Html. You\textquotesingle{}ll need to update your tests to not use these methods.
\item Protractor node module no longer has a config.\+json file. This is now handled in the webdriver-\/manager node module and the files are also downloaded to the webdriver-\/manager/selenium folder.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33136}{}\doxysubsection{Bug fixes}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33136}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/d6910c168550da590b3d4db42f5c853e81cf83b6}{\texttt{ d6910c1}}) fix(edge)\+: Use reset\+Url about\+:blank for Microsoft\+Edge (\#3267)
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/f2055181e60fd358c1764fe716af3d64fc64810b}{\texttt{ f205518}}) fix(launcher)\+: resolve promise for get\+Multi\+Capabilities (\#3195)

closes \#3191
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/f149bd1e91e749a77e8ee147fdb3881584ae6851}{\texttt{ f149bd1}}) fix(docs)\+: Change extension for docs links to .ts (\#3187)

closes \#3170
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/67474e05e73d3facead7c60150c18a2d866185c7}{\texttt{ 67474e0}}) chore(config\+Parser)\+: allow non-\/glob file pattern (\#2754)

Cucumber allows line numbers to be passed in the filename in the form of {\ttfamily features/some.\+feature\+:42}. Glob expanding that results in an empty array and nothing being passed to the framework runner. This change checks for glob magic characters and only tries expanding it if found. Otherwise it just passes the filename verbatim. This was previously handled in \mbox{[}\#2445\mbox{]} by stripping the line number first, but this is a more generic (non-\/cucumber) way to do it. Glob needed to be upgraded for this which resulted in a weird \href{https://github.com/npm/npm/issues/10637}{\texttt{ npm 3 bug}}. Removing the rimraf package resolved this. It was only used to generate documentation which itself was removed a while ago.
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/f311320a1aed09b07d926d0c2aa586202f591b5b}{\texttt{ f311320}}) fix(website)\+: edit get\+Text JSDoc for short\+Description (\#3310)

closes \#3233
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/ba63a92de021193c90794c54fefae39d806fba4a}{\texttt{ ba63a92}}) fix(util)\+: check stack exists before filtering the stack trace (\#3309)

closes \#3224
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/c86acd44bca821491558506964fe1ba8ed5b702a}{\texttt{ c86acd4}}) chore(website)\+: fix website for items to appear properly (\#3314)

\item Replace \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
with 

so descriptions will appear
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/e9b49f24f34730e0648d262be1c410a7f585703a}{\texttt{ e9b49f2}}) fix(config)\+: do not flatten capabilities (\#3291)

This is no longer necessary in the latest version of selenium-\/webdriver. Without this change, {\ttfamily -\/-\/capabilities.\+chrome\+Options.\+binary} will do nothing, for example. Closes \#3290

After this change, you can put multiple browser.\+pause() in the code. Each browser.\+pause() is like a traditional breakpoint.

To detach from the debugger, press $^\wedge$D (CTRL+D). This will continue code execution until it hits the next browser.\+pause() or code finishes running.

This PR also fixes a number of small formatting issues.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/2bde92b3e745e09ad3876932b2d187365e9aaa31}{\texttt{ 2bde92b}}) chore(jasmine)\+: remove jasmine 1.\+3

and update docs. Also, use jasmine 2 for running all Protractor\textquotesingle{}s unit tests.

BREAKING CHANGE\+: Now, both jasmine and jasmine2 frameworks use jasmine 2.\+3. Users still using jasmine version $<$2 will have to upgrade.
\item (\mbox{[}18e1f71\mbox{]}(\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/18e1f71a4dd868709f4e259e05a8a196921e22be}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/commit/18e1f71a4dd868709f4e259e05a8a196921e22be}})) chore(webdriver)\+: upgrade Protractor to webdriver 2.\+48.\+2

BREAKING CHANGE\+: 1) Users will no longer be able to use node versions $<$4. 2) There is significant changes to the control flow, and tests may need to be modified to be compliant with the new control flow. See \href{https://github.com/SeleniumHQ/selenium/blob/master/javascript/node/selenium-webdriver/CHANGES.md}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Selenium\+HQ/selenium/blob/master/javascript/node/selenium-\/webdriver/\+CHANGES.\+md}}
\item (\mbox{[}ac1e21e\mbox{]}(\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/ac1e21e7e09a773de981bf9e70b0fcd489d17a83}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/commit/ac1e21e7e09a773de981bf9e70b0fcd489d17a83}})) chore(plugins)\+: Split first party plugins into seperate repos

BREAKING CHANGE\+:

The Accessibility, Ng\+Hint, Timeline, and Console plugins are now located in their own separate node modules. You will need to explicitly require each module you use. See \href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/blob/master/docs/plugins.md\#first-party-plugins}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/blob/master/docs/plugins.\+md\#first-\/party-\/plugins}} for info for each module.
\item (\mbox{[}ddb8584\mbox{]}(\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/ddb8584a59343284904676ef6d8db5c1c996b900}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/commit/ddb8584a59343284904676ef6d8db5c1c996b900}})) chore(cucumber)\+: Remove cucumber from internal implementation

BREAKING CHANGE\+:

Cucumber has been community maintained for a while, and in order to allow it to move faster, it is no longer part of the core Protractor library. It is now published on npm under \`{}protractor-\/cucumber-\/framework\`{} and will require setting \`{}framework\+Path\`{} in your configuration file. See \href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/blob/master/docs/frameworks.md\#using-cucumber}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/blob/master/docs/frameworks.\+md\#using-\/cucumber}} for full instructions on use now.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33163}{}\doxysection{2.\+5.\+1}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33163}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\mbox{[}9a202ab\mbox{]}(\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/9a202ab5573f24c9919639f1b75fd9cd2b383383}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/commit/9a202ab5573f24c9919639f1b75fd9cd2b383383}})) chore(dependencies)\+: update selenium-\/webdriver to 2.\+47.\+0

Along with it, update \`{}jasminewd2\`{} to avoid situations where the control flow gets locked up and hangs.

$\ast$\+Potential Breaking Change$\ast$\+:

This is passing all existing Protractor tests, but there is a possibility that the changes to the control flow will cause some test flows to hang. If this causes issues, such as tests hanging or commands executing out of order, please revisit your use of functions affecting the control flow, such as \`{}flow.execute\`{}.

See the selenium-\/webdriver changelog at \href{https://github.com/SeleniumHQ/selenium/blob/master/javascript/node/selenium-webdriver/CHANGES.md}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Selenium\+HQ/selenium/blob/master/javascript/node/selenium-\/webdriver/\+CHANGES.\+md}}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\mbox{[}f034e01\mbox{]}(\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/f034e010156a85cf1826b95eb7f41f50ef5a1791}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/commit/f034e010156a85cf1826b95eb7f41f50ef5a1791}})) fix(synchronizing)\+: use the same control flow when ignoring sync

Previously, the order of frames and tasks on the control flow was different depending on \`{}browser.ignore\+Synchronization\`{}. This fixes the inconsistency by creating an empty task when ignore\+Synchronization is true.

Practically, this fixes the polling spec failing after the update to \href{mailto:selenium-webdriver@2.47}{\texttt{ selenium-\/webdriver@2.\+47}}.0.

\item (\mbox{[}c30afdd\mbox{]}(\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/c30afddb80b6138fc5f648f70f2891067d8eeef4}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/commit/c30afddb80b6138fc5f648f70f2891067d8eeef4}})) fix(test)\+: fixed tests under npm test

The bug fix for \#1903 (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/2a765c76e121de13ff86a279fe3f21cb15c17783}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/commit/2a765c76e121de13ff86a279fe3f21cb15c17783}}) was causing Element\+Array\+Finder.\+prototype.\+count to be slow because of the extranous checks that must be performed. fixes(\#2359)
\item (\mbox{[}b147033\mbox{]}(\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/b14703319c0d6bb6a69b76d0fd3732e2ea1fbebc}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/commit/b14703319c0d6bb6a69b76d0fd3732e2ea1fbebc}})) fix(by.\+exact\+Repeater)\+: should split by \char`\"{}=\char`\"{}

Closes \#2335
\item (\mbox{[}4c9886b\mbox{]}(\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/4c9886b410ea4d82098af322044a37908a112138}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/commit/4c9886b410ea4d82098af322044a37908a112138}})) fix(\+Chrome Accessibility Plugin) No error context

If your tests fail because of Stale\+Element\+Reference\+Error then there is no context about where this is coming from. By having the failure be handled inside of the plugin then grunt can fail gracefully. Additionally, this provides context about where the error originated from.

Fixes \#2331
\item (\mbox{[}d15ccdc\mbox{]}(\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/d15ccdcf82bda29c803c3a5642896f16d7e4f938}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/commit/d15ccdcf82bda29c803c3a5642896f16d7e4f938}})) fix(phantom\+JS)\+: Reset URL cannot be a data url for Phantom\+JS

When trying to use the lates version of Angular with Phantom\+JS we get a message complaining about \char`\"{}\+Detected a page unload event\char`\"{}. This was fixed in earlier versions of Angular, see issue \#85, but reappeared now. The problem is that using data urls to reset the page causes this issue, so we have to do as we do with Safari and use \char`\"{}about\+:blank\char`\"{} instead
\item (\mbox{[}e6369ac\mbox{]}(\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/e6369ac973d58a17415ab1211050af26236c6105}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/commit/e6369ac973d58a17415ab1211050af26236c6105}})) docs(tutorial)\+: use Jasmine v2 in the tutorial
\item (\mbox{[}e60dc0f\mbox{]}(\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/e60dc0ff4fc4a6d22e877d4182605913fae5d5cb}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/commit/e60dc0ff4fc4a6d22e877d4182605913fae5d5cb}})) fix(browser.\+refresh)\+: use timeout in milliseconds

When invoked without arguments browser.\+refresh used a 10-\/millisecond timeout, wrongly documented as seconds. It now delegates timeout handling to browser.\+get, which defaults to DEFAULT\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+PAGE\+\_\+\+TIMEOUT (10 seconds).
\item (\mbox{[}0262268\mbox{]}(\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/0262268fa43b9eefac815d986740efa07bb15818}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/commit/0262268fa43b9eefac815d986740efa07bb15818}})) fix(cucumber)\+: fix before\+Feature event handler call guard

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\mbox{[}45341c9\mbox{]}(\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/45341c944bf60537849776c7f362ee0442b219e6}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/commit/45341c944bf60537849776c7f362ee0442b219e6}})) feat(explorer)\+: allow element explorer to start as a server

\item (\mbox{[}cf9a26f\mbox{]}(\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/cf9a26f1b4bdca7d928794d24738786be074619a}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/commit/cf9a26f1b4bdca7d928794d24738786be074619a}})) feat(plugins)\+: allow plugins.\+post\+Test to know what test just ran
\item (\mbox{[}0f80696\mbox{]}(\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/0f806964324cbeb4bceb54c5bd82c639b9f99a49}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/commit/0f806964324cbeb4bceb54c5bd82c639b9f99a49}})) feat(plugins)\+: inline plugins
\item (\mbox{[}de49969\mbox{]}(\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/de499696eb88721cb073a195025ae48f59cbc905}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/commit/de499696eb88721cb073a195025ae48f59cbc905}})) feat(debugger)\+: make element explorer work with node 0.\+12.\+0

Node has changed its debugger significantly in 0.\+12.\+0, and these changes are necessary to get it to work now.

Specifically here are the key points to take note\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Before, the process continues running after \`{}process.\+\_\+debug\+Process(pid);\`{} is called, but now, the process stops. \begin{quote}
To over come this, the call to {\ttfamily process.\+\_\+debug\+Process(pid)} is moved from protractor into the \end{quote}
debugger client. Secondly, because the process stops after the call, we call {\ttfamily req\+Continue} once the debugger connection is established, so that protractor continues into the first break point (for backwards compatibility, we added an extra empty webdriver command so that in earlier versions of node, protractor doesn\textquotesingle{}t go past the first break point from the req\+Continue).
\item Before repl provides \textquotesingle{}(foobar~\newline
)\textquotesingle{} when an user inputs \textquotesingle{}foobar\textquotesingle{}. Now it is just \textquotesingle{}foobar~\newline
\textquotesingle{}. \begin{quote}
We will parse and strip away both the parenthesis and \textquotesingle{}~\newline
\textquotesingle{} to support all versions of node. \end{quote}

\item Additionally (non-\/related to node 0.\+12.\+0), this change makes debugger processes fail fast if the port is taken.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/7b96db0ffb06608b12aa14765133cce42a0cad7f}{\texttt{ 7b96db0}}) feat(browser.\+get)\+: Return a promise that handles errors in browser.\+get
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33182}{}\doxysubsection{Bug Fixes}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33182}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/34f0eebd7e73b10e9b990caa06b63b6fd22b2589}{\texttt{ 34f0eeb}}) fix(element)\+: update to \href{mailto:selenium-webdriver@2.45}{\texttt{ selenium-\/webdriver@2.\+45}}.1 and remove element.\+then

This change updates the version of Web\+Driver\+JS (selenium-\/webdriver node module) from 2.\+44 to 2.\+45.\+1. See the full changelog at \href{https://github.com/SeleniumHQ/selenium/blob/master/javascript/node/selenium-webdriver/CHANGES.md}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Selenium\+HQ/selenium/blob/master/javascript/node/selenium-\/webdriver/\+CHANGES.\+md}}

To enable the update and remove confusion, this removes the {\ttfamily element().then} function unless there is an action result. This function is completely unnecessary, because it would always resolve to itself, but the removal may cause breaking changes.

Before\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{element(by.css('foo')).then(function(el) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  return el.getText().then(...);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\});}

\end{DoxyCode}


After\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{element(by.css('foo')).getText().then(...);}

\end{DoxyCode}


In other words, an Element\+Finder is now no longer a promise until an action has been called.

Before\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{var el = element(by.css('foo'));}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{protractor.promise.isPromise(el); // true}
\DoxyCodeLine{protractor.promise.isPromise(el.click()); // true}

\end{DoxyCode}


After\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{var el = element(by.css('foo'));}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{protractor.promise.isPromise(el); // false}
\DoxyCodeLine{protractor.promise.isPromise(el.click()); // true}

\end{DoxyCode}


Also, fixes {\ttfamily filter} and {\ttfamily map} to work with the new Web\+Driver\+JS.
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/3c048585ac811726d6c6d493ed6d43f6a3570bee}{\texttt{ 3c04858}}) chore(config)\+: remove deprecated {\ttfamily chrome\+Only}

This has been replaced with {\ttfamily direct\+Connect}.
\item Due to (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/1159612ed76bb65612dbb2cc648e45928a251b10}{\texttt{ 1159612}})

Due to changes in how scheduling works on the control flow, specs in Jasmine1 will no longer wait for multiple commands scheduled in {\ttfamily on\+Prepare} or in the global space of the test file.

Before\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{onPrepare: function() \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  browser.driver.manage().window().maximize();}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  // This second command will not finish before the specs start.}
\DoxyCodeLine{  browser.get('http://juliemr.github.io/protractor-\/demo');}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


To fix, return the last promise from on\+Prepare\+:

After\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{onPrepare: function() \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  browser.driver.manage().window().maximize();}
\DoxyCodeLine{  return browser.get('http://juliemr.github.io/protractor-\/demo');}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item Due to (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/1159612ed76bb65612dbb2cc648e45928a251b10}{\texttt{ 1159612}})

Due to changes in Web\+Driver\+JS, {\ttfamily wait} without a timeout will now default to waiting for 0 ms instead of waiting indefinitely.

Before\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{browser.wait(fn); // would wait indefinitely}

\end{DoxyCode}


After 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{browser.wait(fn, 8000) // to fix, add an explicit timeout}

\end{DoxyCode}


This will be reverted in the \href{https://github.com/SeleniumHQ/selenium/blob/master/javascript/node/selenium-webdriver/CHANGES.md\#v2460-dev}{\texttt{ next version of Web\+Driver\+JS}}.

\DoxyCodeLine{  \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\DoxyCodeLine{// do other things}

Now, instances of the {\ttfamily browser} object have a {\ttfamily get\+Processed\+Config} method which returns a promise that resolves to the current Protractor configuration object for the current runner instance. This means that if multi\+Capabilities are being used or tests are sharded, {\ttfamily get\+Processed\+Config} will return an object with the {\ttfamily capabilities} and {\ttfamily specs} property specific to the current instance.

Jasmine2.\+x may now be used by setting {\ttfamily framework\+: jasmine2} in your config. See \href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/blob/master/docs/jasmine-upgrade.md}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/blob/master/docs/jasmine-\/upgrade.\+md}}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/0b930035905d1868225667de358222e51394f3ac}{\texttt{ 0b93003}}) feat(jasmine2)\+: add \textquotesingle{}grep\textquotesingle{} option to jasmine2

Allow users to filter the specs that they want to run using simple string match. To use this feature, either\+: 1) specify jasmine\+Node\+Opts.\+grep in your conf.\+js file or 2) via commandline like \char`\"{}protractor conf.\+js -\/-\/grep=\textquotesingle{}pattern to match\textquotesingle{}\char`\"{}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/4368842da73d4ed501df21b61daf71951e59524b}{\texttt{ 4368842}}) feat(wddebugger)\+: enable repl (with autocomplete) for browser.\+pause

See \href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/blob/master/docs/debugging.md}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/angular/protractor/blob/master/docs/debugging.\+md}} for usage.
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/9c9ed31591f5a3c552222ad7feb1ecd650973902}{\texttt{ 9c9ed31}}) feat(launcher)\+: allow multicapabilities to take array of promises

Enables adding {\ttfamily get\+Multi\+Capabilities\+: function()\{\}} to your configuration file. The function returns either multi\+Capabilities or a promise of a multi\+Capabilities that is resolved after {\ttfamily before\+Launch} and before driver set up. If this is specified, both capabilities and multi\+Capabilities will be ignored.

Also allows specifying {\ttfamily selenium\+Address} in the capabilities/multi\+Capabilities object, which will override the global {\ttfamily selenium\+Address}. This allows you to use a different {\ttfamily selenium\+Address} per capabilities.

Breaking Changes\+: {\ttfamily capabilities} can no longer be a promise. Use get\+Multi\+Capabilities if you need to return a promise. {\ttfamily selenium\+Address} can no longer be a promise. Likewise, use get\+Multi\+Capabilities.
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/167038499aacfd5def03472f9f548529b273e1e0}{\texttt{ 1670384}}) feat(runner)\+: allow protractor to restart browser between tests

Enables adding {\ttfamily restart\+Browser\+Between\+Tests\+: true} to your configuration file. Note that this will slow down test suites considerably. Closes \#1435
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/56beb24b9473ceedc491f3ca00fbce1bb9a18f29}{\texttt{ 56beb24}}) feat(protractor)\+: add browser.\+get\+Registered\+Mock\+Modules()

Now {\ttfamily browser.\+get\+Registered\+Mock\+Modules()} returns a list of the functions or strings that have been registered as mock modules. For troubleshooting.

Closes \#1434.
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/5a404c27326fdb130e5d4ac5c4704b4013c78853}{\texttt{ 5a404c2}}) feat(timeline)\+: add timeline plugin

This plugin gathers test timeline information from the protractor test process, the selenium client logs (if available), and sauce labs (if available), and presents the output visually. This improves understanding of where latency issues are in tests. See \#674

Usage\+:

Add the plugin to your configuration file\+:
\end{DoxyItemize}

\DoxyCodeLine{   outdir: 'timelines',}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{    // Optional -\/ if sauceUser and sauceKey are specified, logs from}
\DoxyCodeLine{   // SauceLabs will also be parsed after test invocation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{     sauceUser: 'Jane',}
\DoxyCodeLine{     sauceKey: 'abcdefg'}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Due to (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/9c9ed31591f5a3c552222ad7feb1ecd650973902}{\texttt{ 9c9ed31}}) feat(launcher)\+: allow multicapabilities to take array of promises

Breaking Changes\+: {\ttfamily capabilities} can no longer be a promise. Use get\+Multi\+Capabilities if you need to return a promise. {\ttfamily selenium\+Address} can no longer be a promise. Likewise, use get\+Multi\+Capabilities.

Why is this breaking change not causing a major version bump? This feature was not fully supported previously and we worked with all known users when making the change.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/0bbfd2b6d38392938781d846ad37b5a0fd964004}{\texttt{ 0bbfd2b}}) feat(protractor/runner)\+: allow multiple browser in test

{\ttfamily protractor.\+get\+Instance()} had been unused (replaced by global {\ttfamily browser} in v0.\+12.\+0) and is now removed.

Before\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{var myBrowser2 = protractor.getInstance();}

\end{DoxyCode}


After\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{// In normal tests, just use the exported global browser}
\DoxyCodeLine{var myBrowser2 = browser;}

\end{DoxyCode}


If you are creating your own instance of the Protractor class, you may still use {\ttfamily protractor.\+wrap\+Driver} as before.

\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/adef9b208fcba2a9d60347bda38a3fe3fac6bf50}{\texttt{ adef9b2}}) feat(runner)\+: add a new method of getting browser drivers -\/ direct\+Connect

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/2fbaf52fd59f03929e173ebf760a97de34bf91d4}{\texttt{ 2fbaf52}}) fix(element)\+: use the root element only to find the testability API, not scope searches

In 9a8f45a a change was introduced which made Protractor\textquotesingle{}s custom locators (by.\+binding, by.\+model, etc) use config.\+root\+Element as the root for all their searches. This meant that config.\+root\+Element was used both to specify how to get hold of Angular\textquotesingle{}s injector as well as where to begin searching for elements. This does not work for all cases, for example if a dialog should be searched for elements but is a sibling, not a child, of ng-\/app.

This reverts that change, and uses document as the parent for all searches. This is consistent with the behavior of the native locators by.\+id, by.\+css, and friends, which do not scope their search based on config.\+root\+Element.
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/9db5327e4ada7eb3caa271b394bcda0ba5e8fd62}{\texttt{ 9db5327}}) fix(\+Element\+Finder)\+: Element\+Finder should allow null as success handler. Passes the value to the next in the chain.
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/0858280db156f924ef126c3aaeae6973b8d44067}{\texttt{ 0858280}}) fix(locators)\+: by.\+css\+Containing\+Text now operates on pre-\/transformed text

Previously, the implementation depended on the browser. Now, it will always operate on the text before text-\/transform is applied. Closes \#1217
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/1a4eea4eb89362822dc86be6904c1ddfba95661e}{\texttt{ 1a4eea4}}) fix(elementexplorer)\+: elementexplorer hangs when returning Element\+Finder
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/f4e6b40c597dc1c59dc7eccfe236abcc336a46a9}{\texttt{ f4e6b40}}) fix(runner)\+: webdriver could get into lock when there is async promise
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/cf284b994fb6766c8ab34d0af9b4ccf8fd866bd1}{\texttt{ cf284b9}}) fix(clientsidescripts)\+: by.\+exact\+Binding not working because of regex typo

Closes \#1441

\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/4f1fe68882dedba662752e722b9e7b76bfed19b6}{\texttt{ 4f1fe68}}) feat(runner)\+: Allow on\+Cleanup to accept a file

\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/466b3831569dc28c5fc2be31fbdf96574e57c3f0}{\texttt{ 466b383}}) feat(protractor)\+: allow advanced features for Element\+Array\+Finder

changed Element\+Finder as a subset of an Element\+Array\+Finder.

This enables actions on Element\+Array\+Finders, such as\+: `element.\+all(by.\+css('.foo\textquotesingle{})).click()\`{}

The function {\ttfamily filter} now returns an Element\+Array\+Finder, so you may also do\+: `element.\+all(by.\+css('.foo\textquotesingle{})).filter(filter\+Fn).click()\`{}

or

`element.\+all(by.\+css('.foo\textquotesingle{})).filter(filter\+Fn).last().click()\`{}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/7bd2dde0a6fca8c8481ad68d0683b4f411d611b9}{\texttt{ 7bd2dde}}) chore(angular)\+: upgrade angular to version 1.\+3.

This change updates Protractor\textquotesingle{}s test application from 1.\+2.\+9 to 1.\+3.\+0-\/r0.

There is a significant behind-\/the-\/scenes change in the implementation of locating elements and waiting for the page to be stable. If you are updating your application to Angular 1.\+3, you may run into some changes you will need to make in your tests\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily by.\+binding} no longer allows using the surrounding {\ttfamily \{\{\}\}}. Previously, these were optional. Before\+: `var el = element(by.\+binding('\{\{foo\}\}\textquotesingle{})){\ttfamily  After\+:}var el = element(by.\+binding(\textquotesingle{}foo\textquotesingle{}))\`{}
\item Prefixes {\ttfamily ng\+\_\+} and {\ttfamily x-\/ng-\/} are no longer allowed for models. Use {\ttfamily ng-\/model}.
\item {\ttfamily by.\+repeater} cannot find elements by row and column which are not children of the row. For example, if your template is {\ttfamily $<$div ng-\/repeat=\char`\"{}foo in foos\char`\"{}$>$\{\{foo.\+name\}\}$<$/div$>$} Before\+: `var el = element(by.\+repeater(\textquotesingle{}foo in foos').row(2).column(\textquotesingle{}foo.\+name\textquotesingle{})){\ttfamily  After\+: You may either enclose}\{\{foo.\+name\}\}{\ttfamily in a child element or simply use\+: }var el = element(by.\+repeater(\textquotesingle{}foo in foos\textquotesingle{}).row(2))\`{}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/ee82f9e3d0656b3c88f041f0115743352bc08941}{\texttt{ ee82f9e}}) feat(webdriver-\/manager)\+: ignore ssl checks with --ignore\+\_\+ssl option

Allow ability to ignore SSL checks when downloading webdriver binaries. Usage\+: {\ttfamily webdriver-\/manager update -\/-\/ignore\+\_\+ssl}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/f7c3c370a239218f6143a4992b1fc4763f4cdd3d}{\texttt{ f7c3c37}}) feat(webdriver)\+: update to Web\+Driver\+JS 2.\+43.\+5

Breaking Changes Web\+Driver\+JS has introduced changes in the way that Promises are handled in version 2.\+43. See \href{https://github.com/SeleniumHQ/selenium/blob/master/javascript/node/selenium-webdriver/CHANGES.md}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Selenium\+HQ/selenium/blob/master/javascript/node/selenium-\/webdriver/\+CHANGES.\+md}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily webdriver.\+Web\+Element} has now been split into {\ttfamily webdriver.\+Web\+Element\+Promise} and {\ttfamily webdriver.\+Web\+Element} so that it does not resolve to itself. This change should be largely transparent to users.
\item {\ttfamily Web\+Element.\+to\+Wire\+Value} has been removed.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/9a8f45af49633f1637c88960ba079d7d425ca72c}{\texttt{ 9a8f45a}}) fix(locators)\+: locators should use the root element provided in config

Previously, locators used \textquotesingle{}document\textquotesingle{} as the root for their search. After this change, they will use the root element provided in the config file -\/ {\ttfamily config.\+root\+Element}. This will make sure behavior is correct if there are multiple angular apps on one page, and also enables the get\+Testability path, because that requires a root element under an ng-\/app.

\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/0c4a70e0ffbbf4373dbd9f1ab29daabe9338d57b}{\texttt{ 0c4a70e}}) fix(protractor) fix stack traces for Web\+Element errors

When angular/protractor@3c0e727136ab3d397c1a9a2bb02692d0aeb9be40 refactored {\ttfamily element()} into the Element\+Finder object, the function lost some of its error handling. This removed references to frames inside tests ({\ttfamily it()} blocks), making it hard to tell where the error was actually occurring.

This commit fixes these problems, showing full stack traces for Web\+Element errors.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/51a5e89f7dace45e61d8eab70e1ea6e9354d4de6}{\texttt{ 51a5e89}}) feat(config)\+: allow setting the get page timeout globally from the config

To change the timeout for how long a page is allowed to stall on {\ttfamily browser.\+get}, change {\ttfamily get\+Page\+Timeout\+: timeout\+\_\+in\+\_\+millis} in the configuration. As before, you may also change the timeout for one particular {\ttfamily get} call by using a second parameter\+: {\ttfamily browser.\+get(url, timeout\+\_\+in\+\_\+sec)}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33230}{}\doxysubsection{Bug Fixes}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33230}

\begin{DoxyItemize}

Closes \#1043
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33231}{}\doxysubsection{Breaking Changes}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33231}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/51a5e89f7dace45e61d8eab70e1ea6e9354d4de6}{\texttt{ 51a5e89}}) feat(config)\+: allow setting the get page timeout globally from the config

This change contains a small breaking change for consistency. Previously, the second parameter to {\ttfamily get} changed the timeout in seconds. Now, the units are milliseconds. This is consistent with all the other timeouts, as well as base Java\+Script functions like set\+Timeout.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item before\+: {\ttfamily browser.\+get(url, 4)}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/56daa54e2e269064bd44bc05ed0bbf2c44657ca8}{\texttt{ 56daa54}}) fix(clientsidescripts)\+: convert non-\/\+Error exceptions to Errors

If any functions called by client\+Side\+Scripts throws a an exception that doesn\textquotesingle{}t inherit from {\ttfamily Error}, the stack trace is completely unhelpful and the message is just \char`\"{}unknown error.\char`\"{} This commit wraps such errors into {\ttfamily Error} instances so that we have meaningful stack traces and the correct exception message.\+ (e.\+g. This is the common case when running dart2js code.\+ This commit gives us the Dart stack trace and exception message.)

In addition, I\textquotesingle{}ve pushed the construction of the string to install into the browser into clientsidescripts.\+js.
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/00c6abef16c47868974eed8ad1a4c38494b2a504}{\texttt{ 00c6abe}}) fix(element)\+: fix Web\+Element.\$ using the incorrect By object

\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/c8c85e0d94d7a7211b000650f01af714663611ad}{\texttt{ c8c85e0}}) fix(locators)\+: fix by.\+repeater finding all rows for IE

Previously, element.\+all(by.\+repeater(\textquotesingle{}foo in foos\textquotesingle{})) would find non-\/element nodes for ng-\/repeat-\/start elements, which could cause IEDriver to fall over if the test tried to get text from those nodes.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/3c0e727136ab3d397c1a9a2bb02692d0aeb9be40}{\texttt{ 3c0e727}}) refactor(protractor)\+: reorganize internal structure of element\+Finder/webelement
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Allow chaining of actions (i.\+e. `element(By.\+x).clear().send\+Keys(\textquotesingle{}abc')\`{})
\item first(), last(), and get(index) are not executed immediately, allowing them to be placed in page objects
\item Rework the way that element\+Finder and wrapped\+Web\+Element is represented
\item Breaking changes\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item element.\+all is chained differently \`{}\`{}\`{} Before\+: element(By.\+x).element.\+all(By.\+y) Now\+: element(By.\+x).all(By.\+y)

However, using element.\+all without chaining did not change, i.\+e. {\ttfamily element.\+all(By.\+x)} \`{}\`{}\`{}
\item Changed the way for retrieving underlying web\+Elements \`{}\`{}\`{} Before\+: element(By.\+x).find(), element(By.\+x).find\+Element(By.\+y), and element(By.\+x).find\+Elements(By.\+y) Now\+: element(By.\+x).get\+Web\+Element(), element(By.\+x).element(By.\+y).get\+Web\+Element(), and element(By.\+x).element(By.\+y).get\+Web\+Elements(), respectively \`{}\`{}\`{}
\item browser.\+find\+Element returns a raw Web\+Element so \$, \$\$, and evaluate will no longer be available
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/fbfc72bad15667990232bb9ff1da503e03d16230}{\texttt{ fbfc72b}}) feat(launcher)\+: Add support for max\+Session
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item add support for max\+Session and capability-\/specific specs
\item cleaned up launcher (refactored out task\+Scheduler.\+js)
\item Breaking change\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item changed the config to shard test files; also sharding is specific to capabilities now \`{}\`{}\`{} Before\+: config.\+split\+Tests\+Between\+Capabilities Now\+: config.\+capabilities.\+shard\+Test\+Files or config.\+multi\+Capabilities\mbox{[}index\mbox{]}.shard\+Test\+Files \`{}\`{}\`{}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/9e5d9e4abb7d0928e6092a711fda527554994be7}{\texttt{ 9e5d9e4}}) feat(locators)\+: remove deprecated locator APIs

This is a {\bfseries{breaking change}}. The following deprecated Locator APIs have been removed.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily by.\+input}
\item {\ttfamily by.\+select}
\item {\ttfamily by.\+selected\+Option}
\item {\ttfamily by.\+textarea}
\end{DoxyItemize}

{\ttfamily input}, {\ttfamily select}, and {\ttfamily textarea} can be replaced by {\ttfamily by.\+model}.

`element(by.\+selected\+Option(\textquotesingle{}foo')){\ttfamily can be replaced by }element(by.\+model(\textquotesingle{}foo\textquotesingle{})).\$(\textquotesingle{}option\+:checked\textquotesingle{})\`{}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33253}{}\doxysection{0.\+23.\+1}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33253}

\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/8b088fd6bf83696fd2ad294d8818e20894332693}{\texttt{ 8b088fd}}) feat(locators)\+: Added a By.\+css\+Containing\+Text locator.

This new locator find elements by css selector and inner text in response to the lack of \textquotesingle{}\+:contains\textquotesingle{} selector.

Example\+: By.\+css\+Containing\+Text(\textquotesingle{}ul .pet\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}Dog\textquotesingle{}) will find all ul children with class \textquotesingle{}pet\textquotesingle{} containing the text \textquotesingle{}Dog\textquotesingle{}.

Closes \#488, Closes \#709
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/54060b7cef4eb2f4c184c360cef7c2eb25c0ff6a}{\texttt{ 54060b7}}) feat(protractor)\+: add the browser.\+set\+Location method to perform in-\/page navigation

Allow a faster way to navigate within the app. The current browser.\+get method forces the entire app to load every time you navigate to a new page. The proposed browser.\+set\+Location method uses the same format as \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesetup_afc13124aa5c0124e84e1d965e3f4b0fb}{\$location.\+url()}}.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/05eb42bb482c7cb36b48af1a86210afc442aa112}{\texttt{ 05eb42b}}) refactor(locators)\+: moves scope in locators to last argument

scope defaults to document, and is an optional argument so now be moved to the end. Came up from debugging and trying to use window.\+client\+Side\+Scripts.\+find\+Inputs(\textquotesingle{}username\textquotesingle{}); which failed. Refactored to match original intent.

BREAKING CHANGE\+: anything relying on clientsidescripts should no longer pass element scope as first argument.

Before\+:

window.\+client\+Side\+Scripts.\+find\+Inputs(document, \textquotesingle{}username\textquotesingle{});

After\+:

window.\+client\+Side\+Scripts.\+find\+Inputs(\textquotesingle{}username\textquotesingle{}, document); // or simply window.\+client\+Side\+Scripts.\+find\+Inputs(\textquotesingle{}username\textquotesingle{});

Also, any custom locators using add\+Locator will now break since the arguments order has changed. To migrate the code follow the example below\+:

Before\+:

var find\+Menu\+Item = function() \{ var dom\+Scope = arguments\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}; var my\+Arg = arguments\mbox{[}1\mbox{]}; // balh blah blah \}; by.\+add\+Locator(\textquotesingle{}menu\+Item\textquotesingle{}, find\+Menu\+Item);

After\+:

var find\+Menu\+Item = function() \{ var my\+Arg = arguments\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}; var dom\+Scope = arguments\mbox{[}1\mbox{]}; // balh blah blah \}; by.\+add\+Locator(\textquotesingle{}menu\+Item\textquotesingle{}, find\+Menu\+Item);

Closes \#497
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33274}{}\doxysection{0.\+18.\+1}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33274}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/a75fa04a70f64e0da29b9a0a9100bd60d9ebf93f}{\texttt{ a75fa04}}) docs(readme)\+: add the travis status widget
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/478c00a01dc9b93de68983b6ef2dfa55f0b42649}{\texttt{ 478c00a}}) feat(runner)\+: add beta support for using mocha as your test framework

This change adds limited support for using mocha as the test framework instead of jasmine. Make the switch by using {\ttfamily -\/-\/framework=mocha} on the command line or adding `framework\+: \textquotesingle{}mocha'\`{} to the config. Tests will be run using the BDD interface. The interface is adapted so that tests run asynchronously without needing to call {\ttfamily done()}.

Note that there is currently no support for an assertion framework, so you will need to require whichever assertion framework you prefer. This means there is no adapter to make the assertions unwrap promises, so you will need to resolve promises yourself and run the assertions afterwards.
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/3731abf901c4278b4470336c3a58765161b08bcc}{\texttt{ 3731abf}}) feat(webdriver-\/manager)\+: add selenium\+Port command line option

Added selenium\+Port command line option so that the standalone selenium server can be started with the supplied port number as opposed to the default port 4444. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\$ webdriver-\/manager start -\/-\/seleniumPort 4443}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33284}{}\doxysubsection{Bug Fixes}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33284}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/478c00a01dc9b93de68983b6ef2dfa55f0b42649}{\texttt{ 478c00a}}) feat(runner)\+: add beta support for using mocha as your test framework

To allow the user to customize their framework, the protractor runner will now wait until just before {\ttfamily on\+Prepare} to load the framework. This means that {\ttfamily jasmine} will not be available in global until {\ttfamily on\+Prepare}. For example, this means that requiring the jasmine-\/reporters module must be done inside on\+Prepare, since that module expects jasmine to be available at the time it is loaded.

{\itshape Note\+: Major version 0 releases are for initial development, and backwards incompatible changes may be introduced at any time.}\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33290}{}\doxysubsection{Features}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33290}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/c579a1a01bae6798a87a5ca8915417775e1b6fb2}{\texttt{ c579a1a}}), (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/f54fd5d7c3caa8df319a0115086bb4db8443d856}{\texttt{ f54fd5d}}) feat(webdriver-\/manager)\+: redo the script to run and install selenium/webdriver

Breaking Change. As outlined in Issue \#296, redoing the way the selenium/webdriver install and run helper scripts work. Now, the \textquotesingle{}webdriver-\/manager\textquotesingle{} script will be available either locally or globally (depending on how protractor was installed). It replaced install\+\_\+selenium\+\_\+standalone and the \textquotesingle{}start\textquotesingle{} script that was provided after install. Run {\ttfamily webdriver-\/manager update} to download new versions of selected webdriver binaries. Run {\ttfamily webdriver-\/manager start} to start the standalone server. In addition, this fixes issues with running the server starter in Windows, and allows automated downloading of the IEDriver.

Thanks to kurthong and vipper for their PRs with windows fixes, which were very useful in preparing this.

If you were calling the tests from somewhere other than the same directory as the config location, you will need to change the paths of selenium\+Server\+Jar and/or chrome\+Driver. Closes \#222.

\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/8580c0c76c5ccd3c55d053e59d8df37b3c4cf35a}{\texttt{ 8580c0c}}) fix(install-\/selenium)\+: update to chromedriver 2.\+6

\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/8ff47875488647513f4199bab36e3b0023dd305d}{\texttt{ 8ff4787}}) fix(runner)\+: exit with proper code when tests fail

When errors with messages matching /timeout/ were created, Protractor clears the control flow so that the remainder of the tasks scheduled for that spec don\textquotesingle{}t bleed over into the next spec. This was messing up the promises used in the runner, since they are also webdriver promises. Long term, the runner should {\itshape not} use webdriver promises. For now, fix by having the runner resolve promises directly rather than through chaining, and add a TODO to use promises which aren\textquotesingle{}t connected to Web\+Driver\textquotesingle{}s control flow in the runner.

Closes \#214.
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/81501c5d941cd7edb15439cef7c7a64c0e773e27}{\texttt{ 81501c5}}) fix(clientsidescripts)\+: workaround for IE 8 \char`\"{}async page reload\char`\"{} init problem

Protractor will now ignore elements with the ng-\/bind class that don\textquotesingle{}t have a proper binding on their data, instead of blowing up when encoutering them.

Closes \#165, may fix \#170
