{\itshape Note\+: Major version 0 releases are for initial development, and backwards incompatible changes may be introduced at any time.}

This change introduces major syntax updates. Using the new syntax is recommended, but the old version is still supported for now. Note also that the test application, docs, and example tests have been updated.\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33301}{}\doxysubsection{Features}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33301}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/a2cd6c8baf242a81c4efea1f55249d597de95329}{\texttt{ a2cd6c8}}) feat(syntax)\+: big syntax reboot, expose global \$, \$\$, element, and by
\end{DoxyItemize}

In an effort to make tests more readable and clear, a few more global variables will now be exported.

{\ttfamily browser} is an instance of protractor. This was previously accessed using {\ttfamily protractor.\+get\+Instance}.

{\ttfamily by} is a collection of element locators. Previously, this was {\ttfamily protractor.\+By}.

{\ttfamily \$} is a shortcut for getting elements by css. `\$('.foo\textquotesingle{}){\ttfamily ===}element(by.\+css(\textquotesingle{}.foo\textquotesingle{}))\`{}

All changes should be backwards incompatible, as tested with the new \textquotesingle{}backwardscompat\textquotesingle{} tests.\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33302}{}\doxysubsection{Bug fixes}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33302}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/8c87ae6b430479445744a2f5c8eaca7f5f03d61d}{\texttt{ 8c87ae6}}) fix(on\+Prepare)\+: on\+Prepare with a string argument should resolve from the config directory
\end{DoxyItemize}

on\+Prepare can take a string, which is a filename containing a script to load adn execute before any tests run. This fixes the string to resolve the filename relative to the config file, instead of relative to the current working directory where protractor is called.\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33303}{}\doxysection{0.\+11.\+0}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33303}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/02cb8199d89c6645d0bc9dbb39e5cb27517bfaf3}{\texttt{ 02cb819}}) feat(cli)\+: allow passing params directly to your test
\end{DoxyItemize}

Adds a config object \textquotesingle{}params\textquotesingle{} which is passed directly to instances of protractor. \textquotesingle{}params\textquotesingle{} may contain nested objects, and can be changed via the command line as\+:

--params.\+login.\+user \textquotesingle{}Joe\textquotesingle{} --params.\+login.\+password \textquotesingle{}abc\textquotesingle{}

This change also switches to using optimist to parse command line flags for more flexibility and better usage documentation. Closes \#32.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/421d6232fe0b45ca1758afd634997da644f2e1db}{\texttt{ 421d623}}) fix(repeat)\+: use 0-\/based indexing for repeater rows
\end{DoxyItemize}

BREAKING CHANGE\+: Finding rows with protractor.\+By.\+repeater now indexes from 0 instead of 1. This should be more familiar to most modern programmers. You will need to edit existing tests. Closes \#90.

Before\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{// The fourth foo}
\DoxyCodeLine{ptor.findElement(protractor.By.repeater('foo in foos').row(4));}

\end{DoxyCode}
 After\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{// The fourth foo}
\DoxyCodeLine{ptor.findElement(protractor.By.repeater('foo in foos').row(3));}

\end{DoxyCode}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/1b7675aab7846bee54117876887bfec07ce31745}{\texttt{ 1b7675a}}) feat(cli)\+: add an on\+Prepare callback to the config
\end{DoxyItemize}

This on\+Prepare callback is useful when you want to do something with protractor before running the specs. For example, you might want to monkey-\/patch protractor with custom functions used by all the specs, or add the protractor instance to the globals. An example usage is shown in the spec/on\+Prepare\+Conf.\+js file and its associated spec.\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33309}{}\doxysubsection{Bug fixes}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33309}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/256b21cf8c744a200892e6b7f9172150b2f4fe8d}{\texttt{ 256b21c}}) fix(cli)\+: allow passing the config file before the options
\end{DoxyItemize}

The cli usage says\+: \begin{quote}
USAGE\+: protractor config\+File \mbox{[}options\mbox{]} \end{quote}
However, the options passed as argument are merged into the default configuration as soon as the config\+File is met in the args parsing loop. This fix merges the options in the default configuration only after the loop, allowing to pass the options to the cli before or after, or around the config file.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/62238252c7fc68c6a5941883f6a272e95997a8ff}{\texttt{ 6223825}}) fix(jasminewd)\+: allow use of custom matchers
\end{DoxyItemize}

Using jasmine.\+Matchers.\+prototype to generate the chained methods for expect() calls is flawed because it does not pick up custom matchers defined using add\+Matcher. Instead, use either the matchers\+Class for the current spec or from the environment.

get\+Current\+Url, get\+Page\+Source, and get\+Title should sync with Angular before executing. Closes \#92.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/0e8de99eb0d8a0db4f6d3538dd051c94f35775f5}{\texttt{ 0e8de99}}) Wrap Web\+Elements with Protractor specific features. This change allows chained find\+Element calls to work with Protractor locators. It also adds a function, evaluate, to evaluate an angular expression in the context of a Web\+Element\textquotesingle{}s scope.
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/9f5311812cbae5122ce2c6ebe522132273b0ebcc}{\texttt{ 9f53118}}) Improving the command line interface (adding more options). This allows the --spec option to be passed with test files that will be resolved relative to the current directory. Smarter merging of default config values. Closes \#65.
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/73821fb6b6d252a93cc15ce990b4ec4738b87b95}{\texttt{ 73821fb}}) Adding an \textquotesingle{}ignore\+Synchronization\textquotesingle{} property to turn off Protractor\textquotesingle{}s attempt to wait for Angular to be ready on a page. This can be used to test pages that poll with \$timeout or \$http.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33313}{}\doxysubsection{Bug fixes}\label{md__home_denis_Documents_Faks_master_RS2_TennisAssociation_TennisAssociation_Client_node_modules_protractor_CHANGELOG_autotoc_md33313}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/cfc6438e80e77387afae776f289cd55813e9b2d9}{\texttt{ cfc6438}}) Adding support for is\+Element\+Present with Protractor locators. Closes \#11.
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/8329b01865074c32f7a261fe9bbf2c151b704a34}{\texttt{ 8329b01}}) Adding wait\+For\+Angular calls before Web\+Element functions. Closes \#37.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/796691205795d93fe12c998d20a58c8220ac6fb7}{\texttt{ 7966912}}) Updating to Selenium 2.\+24.
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/90f0a942b09faff5924674a20ce7705b6d685eba}{\texttt{ 90f0a94}}) Instead of having tests run with the protractor runner need to require() the protractor library, publish it to the global namespace. This insures the instance of protractor used within the tests is the same as the one used on the command line. Closes \#36. Version bump for incompatible API changes.
\item (\href{https://github.com/angular/protractor/commit/cb373c99a7e33c5514bf1d2728a64f631ec8784c}{\texttt{ cb373c9}}) Adding glob matching to the spec files from the config. Closes \#29.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Now running on selenium 2.\+24. Requires updating Web\+Driver\+JS and the selenium standalone binary.
\item The protractor runner now publishes {\ttfamily protractor} to the global namespace and sets up the Jasmine-\/\+Web\+Driver adapter. Tests run with this should no longer include
\end{DoxyItemize}
